1b2(mdo): bod skad du/ 'phags pa rgya tshor rol pa zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo// bim
1b3(mdo): dang po// sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// / 
1b4(mdo): 'di skad bdag gi sa thos pa dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das minyan yod na// 
1b5(mdo): rgyal bu rgyal byed kyi tshal mgon med zas sbyin gyi kuni dga' ra ba na/ dge slong
2a1(mdo): kri nyis stong gi dge slong gi dge 'dun chen po la 'di lta ste/ tshe dang ldan pa kun shes
2a2(mdo): kauN+Di n+ya dang / tshe dang ldan pa rta rdul dang / tshe dang ldan brlangs pa dang / tshe dang ldan pa ming chen dang /

2a4(mdo): lag bzangs dang / tshe dang ldan pa gang po dang / tshe dang ldan pa ba lang bdag dang / tshe dang ldan pa lteng rgyas
2a5(mdo): 'od srung dang / tshe dang ldan pa chu klung 'od srung dang / tshe dang ldan pa g.ya 'od srung dang / tshe dang ldan pa shA
2a6(mdo): de'i bu dang / tshe dang ldan pa maud gal gyi bu chen po dang / tshe dang ldan pa 'od srung chen po dang / tshe dang
2b1(mdo): ldan pa kA t+yA'i bu chen po dang / tshe dang ldan pa ka bi na chen po dang / tshe dang ldan pa gsus po che dang / tshe dang ldan pa skul byed dang / tshe dang ldan pa byams ma'i bu gang po dang / tshe dang ldan
2b2(mdo): pa ma 'gags pa dang / tshe dang ldan pa dga' byed dang / tshe dang ldan pa 'ug pa dang / tshe dang ldan pa rab 'byor dang / tshe dang ldan pa nam gru dang / tshe dang ldan pa song ldeng nags pa dang / tshe dang ldan pa don
2b3(mdo): bod rgyal po dang / tshe dang ldan pa pha rol tu 'gro ba chen po dang / tshe dang ldan pa bkru la dang / tshe dang ldan pa dga' bo dang / tshe dang ldan pa sgra gcan cid dang / tshe dang ldan pa legs 'ongs dang / chong
2b4(mdo): ldan pa kun dka' bo dang / de dag la sogs pa dge slong khri nyis stong dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs so// byang chub sems dpa' sum gri nyis stong pa thams cad kyang skye ba gcig gis thogs
2b5(mdo): byang chub sems dpa'i pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad las nges par skyes pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i mngon par shes pa thams cad kyis rnam par rtse ba/ byang chub sems dpa'i
2b6(mdo): gzungs thams cad thob pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i spobs pa thams cad thob pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam thams cad shin tu yongs su rdzogs pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i so so// 
2b7(mdo): yang dag par rig pa thams cad rtogs par khong du chud pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin thams cad la dbang thob pa/ byang chub sems dpa' dbang thams cad thob pa/ byang chub// 
2b8(mdo): sems dpa'i bzod pa thams cad la zhugs pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa thams cad rab tu rdzogs pa sha stag ste/ 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byams pa dang / 
3b1(mdo): kos paltar thams cad du ma chags ma gos par bzhugs so// bcom ldan 'das kyi grags pa dang / sgra dang snyan pa ni 'di skad du/ bcom ldan 'das de ni de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom
3b2(mdo): pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rig pa dang zhabs su ldan pa/ bde bar gshegs pa/ 'jig rten mkhyen pa/ skyes bu 'dul ba'i kha yo sgyur ba bla na med pa/ lha dang mi rnams kyi ston
3b3(mdo): pa/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das shes bya bar 'jig rten du mngon par grags par gyur to// de ni spyan lnga dang ldan pa ste/ 'jig rten 'di dang 'jig rten pha rol lha dang bcas pa/ tshangs pa dang / 
3b4(mdo): bcas pa/ dge sbyong dang bram zer bcas pa'i skye dgu lnga dang mir bcas pa dag/ rang gis mngon par mkhyen pas mngon du mdzad nas nye bar bsgrubs te rab tu ston to// de thog mar dge ba/ 
3b5(mdo): bar du dge ba/ tha mar dge ba/ don bzang po// tshig 'bru bzang po/ ma 'dres pa/ yongs su rdzogs pa/ yongs su dag pa/ yongs su dkar ba'i chos ston te/ tshangs pa'i spyod pa yang dag par ston/ 
3b6(mdo): to// de'i tshe bcom ldan 'das kyis nam gyi gung thun la/ sangs rgyas kyi rgyan bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs par gyur to// bcom ldan 'das kyis sangs rgyas kyi rgyan
3b7(mdo): bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin de la snyoms par zhugs ma thag tu/ skad cig de nyid la bcom ldan 'das kyi dbu'i gtsug gi gtsug tor gyi gseb nas/ sngon gyi sangs rgyas rjes su dran
3b8(mdo): par bya ba la chags pa med pa'i ye shes snang ba zhes bya ba'i 'od zer byung ste/ des gnas gtsang ma'i lha'i gnas thams cad snang bar byas nas lha'i bu dbang phyug chen po la sogs pa lha'i bu
4a1(mdo): med pa dag yang dag par bskul te// de bzhin gshegs pa'i nod rje gyi tshogs de las bskul pa'i tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag kyang byung ngo // ye shes 'od ldan phur
4a2(mdo): bcom 'od mdzad pa// 'od bzang gzi brji dam pa dri med pa// sku lus bani thugs dge ni 'apo// shAkya'i seng ge thub deng phrad par gyis// ye shes rgya mtsha mthu chen dag pa ste// chos kyi mang
4a3(mdo): bdag kun mkhyen thub pa'i dbang // mi dang lhas mchod lha yi lhar gyur pa// chos la rang byung mnga' dbang mdzad la ston// gang zhig gdul ki'i sems la mnga' mdzad de// gang zhig bdud
4a4(mdo): snyi las grol ba'i thugs// de 'dir mthong thos don med ma yin gyis// rnam grol mthar phyir zhi ba'i drung du deng // mtshungs med thos la snang bar gyur pa ste// mun sel tshul bzang stod
4a5(mdo): par rab mdzad pa// sangs rgyas spyod ni mkhyen pa dpag med pa// de yi drung du dad pa mchog gis deng // de nas sman pa'i rgyal po bdud rtsi gtong // de ni smra ba dpa' bo tsho gas ngan 'joms/ 
4a6(mdo): dechos kyi rtsa lag don dam mkhas// don 'dren pa bla med lam ston pa'o// gnas gtsang ma'i ris kyi lha'i bu de dag sngon gyi sangs rgyas rjes su dran par bya ba la chags pa med pa'i ye she
4a7(mdo): snang ba'i 'od zer des phog cing tshigs su bcad pa rnam pa de lta bu de dag gis kyang bskul ma thag tu rab tu zhi ba'i ting nge 'dzin de las langs nas sangs rgyas kyi mthus bskal pa grangs
4a8(mdo): de tshad med/ bgrang ba lnga shin tu 'dra ba dag las 'das pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams rjes su dran zhing / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gi sangs rgyas kyi zhing
4b1(mdo): gi yon tan bkod pa gang yin pa dag dang / 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor gang yan pa dag dang / chos bstan pa gang yin pa de dag thams cad kyang rjes su dran par gyur to// de nas don rubam mnyam
4b2(mdo): tsam na gnas gtsang ma'i ris kyi lha'i bu dbang phyug ces bya ba dang / dbang phyug chen po dang / dga' bo dang / shin tu dga' bo dang / tsan+dar dang / mchod byas dang / rang ni dang / dul bar 'i
4b3(mdo): dbang phyug la sogs pa de dag dang / gnas gtsang ma'i ris kyi lha'i bu gzhan shin tu mang po kha dog 'phags shing shin tu 'phags dang ldan pa dag gis/ lha'i snang ba rgyal 'u rtsal byed
4b4(mdo): tshal byams cad snang bar byas te/ bcom ldan 'das gal 'ded do rnaMs phyin pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyi na na thos byanag pa gcig tu 'khod do// phyogs gag
4b5(mdo): tu 'khod nas kyang gnas gtsang ma'i ris kyi lha'i bu de dag gis ldan 'das la 'di skad kyi men por to// bcom ldan 'das kyi rer rol bzhes rtsi ba'i chos kyi rnam grangs pado sde
4b6(mdo): shin tu rgyas pa chen po bsdus pa/ byang chums mad rnams kyi dgos pa gang dag pa / dgas kyi brang dam paras 'byung ba dang / dadu dgengs te snyams
4b7(mdo): ga pa'i rnam par rol pa dang / mangs kyi gnas kyi khyad pa kur tu bsgyur pa/ rigs pa po phyir spyod pa mas cad las yod tan gyi byud
4b8(mdo): kyis shin tu 'da' ba bstan pa 'jig rten pa kha zo'i gnas dang / las kyi gnas dang / yi ge dang / grangs dang / lag rtsis dag rtsis dang / ram gri'i thongs dang / 'phong dang / stobs dang kyad kyi
5a1(mdo): 'don sbyangs rnams sems can thams cad las kyang par du 'phags pa kun tu bstan pa/ btsun mo'i 'khor dang / yus gyi longs spyod dang / yongs su spyod ba kun tum
5a2(mdo): pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad kyi su 'thun pas yongs su grub pa'i 'bras bu brnyes pa yongs su brjod pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par ril pa dang / bdud kyin kyil 'khor
5a3(mdo): thams cad rnam par 'jig pa bstan pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs dang / mi 'jigs pa bsdus pa/ sangs rgyas kyi chos tshad ma mchis pa nges par bstan pa/ sngon gyi de bzhin gshegs
5a4(mdo): rnams kyis sngon dud gsungs ma sa te/ 'di sa ste/ bcom ldan 'das pahU~M zla ma dang / chos kyi tog dang / ma yang dang / yon tan gyi tog dang / yon tan 'byung gnas dang / 'ad ra
5a5(mdo): chen po dang / drang srong lha dang / dpal gyi gzi brjid dang / bden pa'i tog dang / rdo rje mkhregs dang / thams cad zil gyis gnon dang / gser mdog dang / shin tu mthor gshegs dang / byi ru'i rgyam
5a6(mdo): dang / me tog gi tog dang / gzugs bzang dang / spyan bzang dang / drang srong skad dang / dmag tshogs las rgyal dang / mtho ba dang / me tog rgyas pa dang / mdzod spu gzi brjid dang / shin du rgyas pa
5a7(mdo): 'od zer bzang po dang / bkra shis ldan dang / bltan bzang dang / seng ge'i gzi brjid chen po dang / blo gros brtan pas byin dang / sos ka'i spros dri dang / bden pa'i chos grags rgya chen dang
5a8(mdo): 'od ldan dang / skar rgyal dang / 'jig rten mdzes dang / 'od rgya chen dang / rin chen grags dang / drag yul gzi brjod dang / rin chen gzi brjid dang / tshangs pa'i gzi brjid dang / sgrasan
5b1(mdo): dang / me tog bzang po dang / re rab me tog dang / rab tu yid 'ong dbyangs dang / dge ba tshul bzangs dang / rab tu 'dzum pa'i spyan dang / yon tan phung po dang / 'brug skra dang // kha dog mdzes dang / rgya
5b2(mdo): brjid dang / ngom bag gang po'i 'gros dang / 'jig rten mngon par smon dag / dgralas rgyal dang / gang dag mchod dang / rnam ra gzigs dang / gtsug ta can dang / thams cad stobs dang
5b3(mdo): 'khor ba 'jigs dang / gser thub dang / de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas 'od srung gis kyang sngon ched gsungs pa lags na/ de bcom ldan 'das
5b4(mdo): gyis kyang skye bo mang po la sman pa dang / skye bo mang po la badre ba dang / 'jig rten la thugs brtse ba dang / skye bo phal po che'i don dang / lha dang me rnams kyi don du 'gyur ba dang / sman pa dang bde ba
5b5(mdo): 'gyur ba dang / theg pa chen po 'di'ang brjod pa dang / phas kyi rgol ba thams cad tshar bcad pa dang / bdud thams cad zil gyis gnon pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la bstan
5b6(mdo): pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa pa'i gang zag thams cad kyi brtson 'grus brtsam pa bskyed pa dang / dam pa'i chos yongs su gzung ba dang / dkon mchog gsum gyi gdung mi bcad
5b7(mdo): ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa yongs su rdzogs pa yang kun tu bstan pa'i slad du da bstan du gsol zhes gsol pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis lci'i bu de dag dang lha dang bcas pa'i
5b8(mdo): 'jig rten la thugs brtse ba'i phyir cang mi gsung bas gnang ngo // de nas lha'i bu de dag kyang / bcom ldan 'das kyis cang mi gsung bas gnang bar rig nas tshim zhing mgu la yi rangs

7b7(mdo): la mkhas pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyis gsung ba gzung ba la dran pa'i snod 'khrul pa med pa dang / gzungs mtha' yas su med pa rab tu thob pa/ dran pa nye bar gzhag pa dang /

8a3(mdo): rdo rje'i mtshon sra ba dang ldan pa/ byang chub kyi sems kyi rtsa ba las snying rje chen po'i chub lhag pa'i bsam pas skyes pa zab cing brtan pa dang / brtson 'grus kyi chos kyi chus mdzan
8a4(mdo): par brlan pa/ thabs mkhas pa'i snying po dang ldan pa/ byang chub kyi yan lag dang / bsam gtan gyi zer ba can/ ting nge 'dzin gyi ze 'bru dang ldan pa/ yon tan gyi tshogs

8b2(mdo): hU~M phyogs kyi mos sum cu rtsa ba ni yang dag par 'arjes su rdzogs pas ral patsud du byas shing rig pa dang / ya shes 'angs can/ rnam par thar pa'i sgrog sa ma kyi la gdapa / 
8b3(mdo): zhi gnas dang lhag mthong shin tu rnam par dag pa'i mig dang ldan pa/ bsam gtan dang / rnam par thar pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / snyoms par 'jug pa'i ri yul gyi phug na gnas
